## [有哪些英文歌的歌词很美或很感人？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/26708731/answer/34283689)
谢邀，  
  
很多我喜欢的因为不适合在这里列出，因为它出色点在技术，旋律，节奏等方面上，而不在歌词上。不过，歌词好的还是有的，下面给大家分享几首。
因为提问针对英文歌词，我觉得对此问题感兴趣的知友应该都能看懂英文，所以下面歌曲列表以及简洁干脆用英文。  
  
列表不是排行榜，而是分类型的。类型不是正常音乐类型（摇滚，爵士，等）而是主题类型。看目录就明白了：  
  
 **Tables of Contents - 目录**  
  
Protest Songs 反抗歌曲  
Social Alienation 社会疏离感歌曲  
Social Commentary Songs 社会评论歌曲  
Wordplay Songs 文字游戏歌曲  
Contemplative Songs 深思歌曲  
Feminist Songs 女权主义歌曲  
Love Songs 爱情歌曲  
Motivational Songs 励志性歌曲  
Nostalgic Songs 怀旧歌曲  
  
 **Protest Songs - 反抗歌曲**  
  
[Edelweiss - The Sound of Music
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770355117%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.Rvrtnx)  
The most delicate song of The Sound of Music, but also very masculine, and my
favorite. Simple lyrics but full of feeling, Captain Von Trapp sings this song
as a love song to his country Austria even as it is taken over by Nazi
Germany.  
  
[Peruvian Cocaine - Immortal Technique
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2213409%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.BWZUJp)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
Immortal Technique is a Latino American rapper with very strong political
content. This song is about the cocaine trade. In it, he criticizes the US
government for its hyprocrisy, fighting a "war against drugs" on the streets
while at the same time supporting right-wing dictators in South America who
profit from the drug trade  
  
[Fortunate Son - Creedence Clearwater Revival
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3422858%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.97.B977bL)  
This is a great rocker, and has powerful political lyrics too. It's about how
during the Vietnam War, most of the soldiers forced to go to Vietnam were
minorities or lower class, while the sons of rich white men were able to avoid
the draft.  
  
[Another Brick in the Wall (Part 2) - Pink Floyd
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2067406%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.gyyecu)  
Not only is this a classic rock song, the lyrics are a masterpiece of dark
cynicism and anti-establishment angst. "We don't need no education, we don't
need no thought patrol". When I was a graduate student, some professors in my
department formed a rock band and played a cover of this song. Don't
misunderstand me. This song is not against knowledge or learning. It's against
dogmatic and narrow-minded education. Think for yourself.  
  
[For What It's Worth - Buffalo Springfield
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3422864%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.25.qCZY46)  
A classic Vietnam War era anthem, in support of the anti-war protestors  
  
[Hurricane - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1772610063%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.24.5rJBYU)  
This song is about an African American boxer who was wrongly accused of murder
and sentenced to prison, even though he was innocent. Bob Dylan sang this song
to try to publicize his plight and seek justice.  
  
[The Times They Are A-Changin' - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1024678%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.gpiKIT)  
When Bob Dylan penned this song back in 1964 he was thinking about the Civil
Right movement, the sexual revolution, the Vietnam War, and all those
momentous social changes. The issues we're invested in today are different,
but the message of the song still applies. The times, they're always a
changin'.  
  
[John Brown - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3596806%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.25.9UPUIx)  
This is one of the best anti-war songs ever written. Bob Dylan tells the story
of John Brown, a young man who is drafted to go to fight in Vietnam. His
mother is so proud of him, and tells all her neighbors that her son is a hero.
But when her son returns from the war, disfigured and torn apart, he tells his
mother that war is wrong, and that when he saw the Vietnamese enemy, "he could
see that his face was just like mine"  
  
[With God on Our Side - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1024680%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.hHDag6)  
Another anti-war song by the great Bob Dylan, but one with a greater
historical scope. Bob Dylan traces all the wars that the United States has
fought throughout history, and points his finger at those who think that the
US has God on its side and is thus justified.  
  
[The Outcast - Dave van Ronk
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2764597%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.WPLDDS)  
This song is speaking for all the immigrants who have been discriminated
against, for all the people who have been oppressed and outcast in American
history. But it's not a sad or angry song. The singer is happy and laughing
the whole time. I think that's what makes this song so interesting. He's
actually proud to be an outcast.  
  
[War - Edwin Starr
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770771946%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.hShdls)  
One of many great anti-war anthems to emerge in opposition to the Vietnam War.
The Vietnam War was terrible, but it did give rise to some great music. "War
…what is it good for? Absolutely nothing!"  
  
[American Idiot - Green Day
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3365853%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.wFDbcK)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
Green Day started off as a childish punk rock group in my home town, but by
2004 they had become a band with a lot more musical and lyrical ideas. They
released this album during the peak of George W. Bush's war on Iraq. The
lyrics are clearly objecting to the mindset of the day, which was to blindly
follow the president and the media.  
  
[Gloria - Patti Smith
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770368387%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.yS0Vax)  
She hits you like a sledgehammer with that first line "Jesus died for
somebody's sins, but not mine." For that, Patti cemented herself as a hero in
the eyes of those determined to stand up against the dogma of conservative
Christianity.  
  
[Redemption Song - Bob Marley
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1529677%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.t2BVRc)  
Reggae's greatest artist, Bob Marley was also a religious man. I don't
normally praise religious lyrics, but this song is an exception. Bob Marley
was a Rastafari, who believe that the the descendants of the people of Israel
settled in Ethiopia in Africa, and that Europeans later whitewashed
Christianity. The best line is "emancipate yourself from mental slavery".  
  
[Do You Hear the People Sing - Les Miserables
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1771335126%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.KiXLaX)  
The great protest song of Les Mis erables, this is where the student protest
leaders join together in unity to fight against what they believe is the
corrupt French government.  
  
[We're Not Gonna Take It - Tommy
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1127223%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.v1NAft)  
This is the last song in the musical Tommy, about a deaf, dumb, and blind boy
who becomes a pinball wizard (basically, a guy who's really good a pinball, an
arcade game). In the process, Tommy attracts a huge following of people
(parodying the religious cults of the 1970s) who want to be just like him, so
Tommy makes them cover their eyes and plug their ears and mouths. But then
they discover that they "can't take it" and sing this song.  
  
 **Social Alienation Songs － 社会疏离感歌曲**  
  
[Hurt - Johnny Cash
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1274569%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.j4q3fl)  
This is a cover of a song by Nine Inch Nails, but I think Johnny Cash does it
better. The country music legend was 70 years old when he covered this
industrial metal song (there aren't many 70 years old doing that). When Trent
Renzor of Nine Inch Nails heard Johnny Cash's cover he said "it's his song
now", that's how powerful it was. This song is dark. It's about pain, and how
humans either try to block it from their memory, or face it and deal with it.  
  
[Not Ready Yet - Eels
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1436103%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.0FkMeM)  
This song is about a man who is shy and lonely and feels alienated from the
world. He wants to join the world but he's just "not ready yet".  
  
[Guest List - Eels
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1436106%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.JsYSXV)  
Another Eels song about Alienation. He wants to be included but he's not on
the "guest list". A lot people can probably relate to this song.  
  
[Creep - Radiohead
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1079377%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.XmFL29)  
I love Radiohead, but mostly for the music. Their lyrics are often sparse.
Creep is an exception, a beautiful song about alienation and not belonging.  
  
[Gollum's Song - Emiliana Torrini
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3408235%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.pdeWgx)  
The music of the Lord of the Rings is beautiful. Most of the songs are
instrumental. The Enya songs at the end of The Fellowship of the Ring and The
Return of the King are good, but the lyrics aren't that special. The lyrics of
this song, however, are haunting. Gollum is my favorite character (one of the
most complex and "human", if you can believe that) and this song is sung from
his perspective. Poor Gollum.  
  
[Bullet With Butterfly Wings - The Smashing Pumpkins
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2079452%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.xo97Wa)  
This song was an anthem of teenagers when I was in middle school. Besides
their style of alternative rock, the Smashing Pumpkins spoke to my generation
with their disaffected, bleak lyrics. One interpretation is that this song is
about trying to make art and music in a world controlled by executives and
media sharks and lawyers.  
  
[Loser - Beck
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1004460%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.8mGdOs)  
The lyrics to this early Beck song are quite ridiculous, but they rhyme and
are terrific fun. For all those Chinese 吊丝, this song is for you! The lyrics,
by the way, were completely improvised. Beck felt embarrassed that they were
so bad that he improvised the line "I'm a loser baby so why don't you kill
me?"  
  
[Add It Up - Violent Femmes
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1311422%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.JVqZCd)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
Experimental alternative rock song about a frustrated teenage virgin who can't
get laid. Who hasn't been there?  
  
[Mad World - Tears for Fears
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3422278%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.Ta4BXw)  
A song about alienation and depression. Haunting lyrics with penetrate into
your soul … "the dreams in which I'm dying are the best I've ever had". Gary
Jules covered this song for the movie Donnie Darko, making it even more dark
and gloomy.  
  
[Comfortably Numb - Pink Floyd
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2067169%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.YgadVJ)  
The most lyrically powerful of Pink Floyd's songs, and sonically gorgeous as
well. Clear drug references, about what happens when you get so lost in a
world of drugs you can't tell the fantasy from reality.  
  
[I Dreamed a Dream- Les Miserables
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769424192%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.36.KXn1Lv)  
From the musical Les Mis erables, a real heartjerker. For Fantine, nothing's
going right for her.  
  
[On My Own-Claude - Les Miserables
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1771497675%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.E9cpd9)  
Also from the musical Les Mis erables, Eponine's showstopper about unrequited
love.  
  
[One Song Glory - Rent
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769558463%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.WpVHcf)  
From the rock musical Rent, Roger's tortured ballad about searching for
meaning in life when he knows he's dying of AIDS.  
  
[Memory - Cats
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768932294%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.kCPNRN)  
From the musical Cats, the last ditch effort of Grizabella, the now washed-up
star, to reclaim her former glory  
  
 **Social Commentary Songs - 社会评论歌曲**  
  
[Dance With the Devil - Immortal Technique
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2213435%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.VwAY8f)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
Another song by Immortal Technique. This one is really heavy content, I don't
recommend it for everyone. It's the story about a boy who is seduced by
materialism and joins a gang and has to commit a terrible crime. The message
of the song is against materialism and violence, but it's intense.  
  
[Liberation - OutKast
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1245810%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.1Eh5Zr)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
One of the more poignant rap songs I've heard. Outkast have always been
lyrical, and the contrast between Andre and Big Boi's style here is used to
maximum effect. A sexy, surreal, and eternally cool song musing on the nature
of fame and materialism.  
  
[Imagine - John Lennon
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1122167%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.W4XwsR)  
This song I'm guessing most of you know. John Lennon is singing about how
religion and materialism and war have created pain and suffering and misery,
and wouldn't life be so much better if we all stopped caring about dogma and
fighting and showing off, and just loving each other instead. Extremely
simple, but truly profound lyrics. John Lennon, wherever you are, I agree with
you.  
  
[7 O'Clock News/Silent Night - Simon & Garfunkel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1283258%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.JE6xUL)  
It's hard not to have chills down your spine when you listen to this song.
Simon & Garfunkel chose a single broadcast of the nightly news, talking about
the Vietnam War and racism, and juxtaposed with with the Christmas song Silent
Night.  
  
[Heroin - The Velvet Underground
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1111797%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.1UrSzC)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
I don't recommend this song for everyone. It's intense and it's about taking
drugs. Heroin, the worst drug of all. Lou Reed, the lead singer of the Velvet
Underground, was a heroin user. These lyrics are his first person account of
what it's like to take this drug. I'm not endorsing use of heroin. But as a
piece of art, this song is pretty powerful.  
  
[Like a Rolling Stone - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1024710%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.DnA172)  
This is Bob Dylan's most famous song. It's about his ex-girlfriend, a
golddigger. Bob Dylan is mocking all those people who are shallow and arrogant
and materialistic.  
  
[Blowin' in the Wind - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1024665%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.gkgYIz)  
Have you noticed that I've included lots of Bob Dylan songs here? That's
because he's one of the greatest songwriters in history. There's so much rich
meaning in this song. "How many times must a man look up before he can see the
sky?" tells us that we're often blind to what's right in front of us. "How
many years can a mountain exist before it's washed to the sea?" makes us
ponder the longevity of our existence on earth. And "how many deaths will it
take till he knows that too many people have died?" is a clear message against
the Vietnam War.  
  
[Apeman - The Kinks
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769051582%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.IfziEn)  
This is a funny song by one of the pioneering groups in rock music, the Kinks.
It's about disillusionment with modern urban life, and how life would be
happier if humans returned to their primitive state in the jungle as "apemen".  
  
[The Ballad of Edward Abbey - Tom Russell
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2764669%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.xr7CDc)  
Tom Russell poignantly tells the tale of Edward Abbey, an American
environmental activist who lived against the grain, a real unique soul. The
critique of suburban housing tracts in the end really rings true.  
  
[God Bless The Child - Billie Holiday
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770219522%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.CslCq5)  
Billie Holiday was one of the greatest female singers in jazz music. The
lyrics of this song are deep and powerful, talking about economic inequality
and the power that money has over people. She sang this back in 1939, during
the Great Depression, but it's message still rings clear and true today in
this new age of economic excess.  
  
[The Lizards - Phish
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769022511%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.j0Y4bF)  
Phish is a great jam band. Mainly I like them for their instrumental music.
But I want to introduce them to you, and the lyrics to this song are pretty
interesting, telling a fantastical story about a strange people called the
Lizards. It's sort of an allegory for a society which doesn't allow freedom of
thinking.  
  
[Jesus the Missing Years - John Prine
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1066118%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.12.MlIf9B)  
This is an example of how not everyone in the US treats Christianity with
terrible seriousness. John Prine noticed that the story of Jesus in the Bible
has a big gap during his youth. So he decided to "fill in" the story with this
funny song.  
  
[Minority - Green Day
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1035325%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.hRf40B)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
An anthem to individuality. Don't be like everyone else. Be different. There's
nothing to be ashamed of being a minority.  
  
[Date Rape - Sublime
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770228604%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.1CeQTJ)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
This song is a warning to guys not to commit date rape. A bit childish, but it
was quite revolutionary at the time (1992) for male musicians to be singing
about such topics. Plus, it's a damn catchy ska song.  
  
[Nothing But Sunshine - Atmosphere
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3459672%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.qpstU2)  
*explicit lyrics warning*  
This rapper has a lot of anger, much of it from his difficult childhood. In
this song he explains why his childhood was messed up, and in the process
confronts his pain and shows that he's dealing with it.  
  
[Sympathy for the Devil - The Rolling Stones
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1271340%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.NkE0YY)  
Easily my favorite Rolling Stones song. When this song came out, a lot of
Christians thought it was evil and satanic. Although it is told from the
perspective of the devil, if you look closely at the lyrics you'll realize
it's actually a very profound song which is not condoning evil, but pointing
out that evil is our own doing. The song lists several historical events, from
the cruxifiction of Jesus Christ, to the murder of the Czar, to the
assassination of John F Kennedy. But the devil points out that it wasn't him
who did these things, it was humans. Same goes for war? Who is responsible for
most wars in human history? Humans, and most of them fighting on behalf of one
"God" or another. Clearly, the real evil in our world is not that of some
fictitious devil, but in ourselves.  
  
[One Tin Soldier - Bushmen
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773073277%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.79.2pTEXI)  
This classic hippie song is about people who live on a mountain who have a
treasure buried underneath a stone, and people who live in the valley who
covet the treasure, so they attack the mountain people and kill them all, but
when they turn the stone over, "Peace on Earth" is all it says. When I was a
kid at summer camp, we used to sing this song and its powerful message has
always stuck with me.  
  
[Cats In The Cradle - Harry Chapin
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1772795152%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.3MnFYp)  
Another song I learned around the campfire at summer camp. A really poignant
story about a boy whose father is always too busy to spend time with him when
he's growing up. Then, when the boy grows up and has a family of his own, and
the father is an and old man and wants to see his son, his son is too busy.
Karma's a bitch.  
  
[Sam Stone - John Prine
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1064779%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.G22ELE)  
A powerful folk song about a soldier who is injured in the Vietnam War, and
becomes addicted to drugs, much to the dismay of his family.  
  
[This Land Is Your Land - Woody Guthrie
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1771179278%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.74.9mS2IK)  
This is a truly great American song. I wish that this were our song were our
national anthem instead of the bombastic wreck of a song we're currently stuck
with. This song is about sharing the bounty of our land and resources with our
brothers and sisters. Woody Guthrie wrote this song during the Great
Depression, and it has clear egalitarian, even socialist, leanings. It speaks
of the beauty of the American continent, and makes it clear that it shouldn't
belong to corporations or millionaires but to you and me.  
  
[Montage, Pt. 1
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1771326340%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.6659513.0.0.IM2s0r)[\-
Chorus Line
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773124679%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.6659513.0.0.IM2s0r)  
[Montage, Pt. 2
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773124684%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.6659513.0.0.IM2s0r)[\-
Chorus Line
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773124679%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.6659513.0.0.IM2s0r)  
[Montage, Pt. 3 - Chorus Line
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773124679%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.6659513.0.0.IM2s0r)  
A Chorus Line is a terrific Broadway musical about actors and dancers
struggling to get jobs on the "chorus line" (i.e. in the background) of a
broad musical. In it they sing about their lives, loves, failures, hopes, and
fears. It's a real slice-of-life musical, and this three-part Montage is one
of the lyrical highlights of the show. Keep in mind, A Chorus Line came out in
1975, so several of the references to celebrities and such are dated today.  
  
[Superstar - Jesus Christ Superstar
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770070151%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.12.CZ6tYi)  
This is my favorite song from the rock musical Jesus Christ Superstar. In this
song, Judas Iscariot is criticizing Jesus for his behavior, and saying he
should have come to Earth two thousand years later when mass communication
would have made his impact much greater.  
  
[America - West Side Story
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2081339%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.fx1aCa)  
This song is song between two groups: The boys of the Puerto Rican gang The
Sharks, and their girlfriends. The girls' lyrics talk about how much they love
life in America (they were recent immigrants at the time), but the boys
respond with the opposite argument, that they are treated like dirt in America
and would rather go back home to Puerto Rico. Sounds like a serious song, but
it's quite fun. For the full effect, you should see the movie. The dance moves
in this Latin number are fantastic.  
  
[Gee, Officer Krupke - West Side Story
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770011574%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.2I2lvq)  
In the musical West Side Story, members of the teenage street gang The Jets
take out their frustrations by singing this comical song in, in which they
purport to beg Officer Krupke not to arrest them, giving excuses for why
they're so bad. In the course of the song, the boys are sent from the police
to the judge, to a psychiatrist, to a social worker, who finally pronounces
them simply "no good"! I was in this musical in high school and played the
Judge in this song. For the full effect, you should watch the movie West Side
Story. The staging of the song is brilliant.  
  
 **Wordplay Songs - 文字游戏歌曲**  
  
[Subterranean Homesick Blues - Bob Dylan
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1024699%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.Ncy5ns)  
These are not Bob Dylan's deepest lyrics, but they are a lot of fun. The music
video is a classic.  
  
[It's the End of the World as We Know It (And I Feel Fine) - R.E.M
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1263014%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.24.Z2FHgH)  
This is one of the most fun songs you'll ever hear. It's a fast song, full of
lyrics, seemingly disconnected. Try to sing along this song in KTV, it's a
real challenge! This song is actually poking fun at students in debate club
who are always trying to say so much in a short period of time, and who tend
to make grand claims such as "if you don't do this ….it's going to be the end
of the world". Well, REM's Michael Stipe's response is "I'm not that worried,
even if it's the "so-called end of the world" I feel fine".  
  
[Alphabet Aerobics - Blackalicious
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770740540%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.23.scTf7s)  
This is a really fun rap song. Each verse makes use of words starting with
each letter of the alphabet, in consecutive order. Blackalicious is brilliant
at word play, and shows that rap music can be intelligent and eloquent. The
song speeds up gradually until he gets to the letter Z.  
  
[Me Gustas Tu - Manu Chao
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2737372%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.uNf9oi)  
Okay, this song isn't English, but it's one of my favorites. Manu Chao is a
Spanish singer, and the lyrics of this are are really simple but really cute
(or, as you like to say, 萌). Here, I'll translate some of them for you:  
"I like airplanes, I like you.  
I like to travel, I like you.  
I like the morning, I like you.  
I like the wind, I like you.  
I like to dream, I like you.  
I like the sea, I like you."  
  
[Rapper's Delight - Sugarhill Gang
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1772193301%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.ik7BIM)  
This was one of the first hit rap songs, back in the early 1980s (before I was
born). At 8 minutes, it's a long song, but it's got a great beat and the raps
are fun and clever. These guys influenced every other rap act that came after.  
  
[I'm Too Sexy - Right Said Fred
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769561483%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.ivx8rX)  
File this one hit wonder in the category of "ridiculous lyrics". Still, one of
the catchiest, most irresistible pieces of pop music ever made.  
  
[I've Been Everywhere - Johnny Cash
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1274363%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.9hyuC3)  
This song is kind of like a geography lesson. Johnny sings about all the
places he's been. He names nearly a hundred different cities in the USA, and
makes them all rhyme.  
  
[Light My Candle - Rent
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769558464%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.fCOP5x)  
This song some of the best lyrics in the rock musical Rent. Roger's power is
out, and the girl down the hall Mimi knocks on his door looking for a candle.
Lots more ensures in this clever, sexy, and funny song.  
  
 **Contemplative Songs - 深思** **歌 曲**  
  
[The Sound of Silence - Simon & Garfunkel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1283216%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.24.Sf7ATd)  
My favorite Simon & Garfunkel song, the lyrics are simply phenomenal. From the
opening line "Hello darkness my old friend" to crescendos like "the words of a
prophets are written on the subway walls" these words move me to no end.  
  
[All Things Must Pass - George Harrison
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1037180%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.XZ9ngI)  
A moving song by my favorite member of the Beatles. George actually wrote this
song when the Beatles were still together but it came out after they broke up.
The song really reflects that period in his career and life, that the Beatles
must come to an end, that all things come to an end eventually, but that life
will go on. Simple lyrics, but beautifully sung.  
  
[Let It Be - The Beatles
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1003989%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.CSK2Um)  
This message of this song is similar to All Things Must Pass, and also comes
at the end of the Beatles' career, but this one is from Paul McCartney. Not as
deep as All Things Must Pass, but the song overall is better, and the lyrics
are easy to remember which makes this a good KTV song.  
  
[While My Guitar Gently Weeps - The Beatles
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1003930%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.TEM6s0)  
Another great George Harrison song. I just love the concept that his guitar is
"weeping". I'll borrow here a line from the top comment on[songmeanings.com
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//songmeanings.com/songs/view/1206/):
"This is an elegy, a lament, for the decadence of the world and society in
general."  
  
[Wish You Were Here - Pink Floyd
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2067148%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.25.DHJdZD)  
A tribute to Syd Barrett, founding member of Pink Floyd, who left the group
due to his heavy drug use and erratic behavior.  
  
[Bang Bang (My Baby Shot Me Down) - Nancy Sinatra
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3409196%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.pCX9au)  
Some of you may recognize this song from the Quentin Tarantino movie Kill
Bill. Nancy Sinatra (Frank Sinatra's daughter) has a haunting, sultry voice.
I'm not sure if the song is actually about death, or lost love, but it sure is
memorable.  
  
[All This Way for the Short Ride - Tom Russell
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2764662%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.5y9ObP)  
This song is about a man who performs trick jumping on horseback. But he has
an accident and dies, leaving behind his wife and unborn child. Moving lyrics
and a gorgeous song by the great Tom Russell.  
  
[You Can't Always Get What You Want - The Rolling Stones
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1271388%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.ljLlP9)  
Another epic Rolling Stones song, starting off with a lone female chorus, and
building into one of the most grandiose rock song in history. The lyrics are
extremely simple but underlie a great truth, that "we can't always get what we
want" and sometimes we should just learn to be content with what we have.  
  
[Landslide - The Smashing Pumpkins
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2382141%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.lYi9qN)  
Another song I learned around the campfire at summer camp. Earnest,
passionate, eloquent. The song was originally Fleetwood Mac's but I like this
Smashing Pumpkins cover better.  
  
[Stars - Les Miserables
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1771497672%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.Z62Dmn)  
From the musical Les Mis erables. We're supposed to root against Inspector
Javert in his pursuit of the wronged hero Jean Valjean, but when he exposes
the meaning behind his quest, we can't help but sympathize with him, too.
Easily the most beautiful song from Les Miserables.  
  
[Soliloquy - Carousel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773010480%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.SxSZL0)  
From the musical Carousel, Billy Bigalow is having a conversation in his own
head about what it's going to be like when his wife has a child. A tour-de-
force 8-minute song which careens from joy to fear and exposes a man's
innermost struggles.  
  
[I've Seen It All - Bjork
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768916324%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.qlExio)  
From the movie Dancer in the Dark, blind Selma is trying to explain that even
though she is going blind, she has seen enough beauty in the world that she
will always treasure it. The video for this song is amazing.  
  
 **Feminist Songs - 女权主义歌曲**  
  
[Doo Wop (That Thing) - Lauryn Hill
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1371216%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.u88k3a)  
Lauryn Hill is one of the best female rappers in history. Lots of her songs
have excellent, meaningful lyrics. I choose this one not because it's the
best, but because it's the most catchy, and the message, about girls
respecting themselves, is a good one.  
  
[That Day - Poe
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2328710%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.iLm1FY)  
This is a song about a woman woman who's been mistreated by men (her
boyfriend? her father?) and is fighting back. A powerful feminist song.  
  
[You Oughta Know - Alanis Morissette
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1216443%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.JMaEhT)  
One of the great female power songs. Alanis Morissette's been dumped by her
boyfriend, and she's pissed …watch out. Girls, if you've ever been dumped, you
can probably relate.  
  
[Whatta Man - Salt-N-Pepa
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2011318%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.7s0Gk4)  
A classic feminist hip hop song, where the girls sing about what kind of man
they like. A man who's cool and sexy, but who also treats women with respect.  
  
 **Love Songs - 爱情歌曲**  
  
[Hallelujah - Rufus Wainwright
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768940062%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.3jmxeZ)  
Rufus Wainwright has a gorgeous voice, and in this cover of Hallelujah he tugs
at your heart strings.  
  
[Elephant Love Medley - Moulin Rouge
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768949738%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.122.v45q3B)  
This song is from the musical film Moulin Rouge. It's a medley of pop songs
--all of them about love--in which the film's two protagonists exchange verses
arguing over the value of true love, before finally singing in unison,
signaling that the prostitute Satine has finally let down her guard and
allowed herself to be swayed by Christian's love.  
  
[You Don't Know My Name - Alicia Keys
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1944910%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.2K0VU7)  
My favorite Alicia Keys song, her voice is so sexy and sultry. Although the
lyrics are simple, the story they tell is a good one. I especially like the
spoken voice section of the song, where she's talking on the phone to the boy
she likes.  
  
[Breakfast At Tiffany's - Deep Blue Something
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2336963%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.N8Ncrx)  
A great alternative rock song from the 1990s, about a guy who's trying to
salvage his relationship with his girlfriend, and reaching for any thread of
something they have in common remembers that they both "kind of liked" that
film Breakfast at Tiffany's with Audrey Heburn, and then crafts a whole song
out of that idea.  
  
[Muzzle - The Smashing Pumpkins
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2079458%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.YjxNYH)  
This was one of my absolute favorite songs when I first heard it in 8th grade,
and it still is today. The first line "I fear that I am ordinary, just like
everyone", followed by that crescendo of a drumroll is what we all fear. The
ending is so poetic:  
"And I knew the meaning of it all  
And I knew the distance to the sun  
And I knew the echo that is love  
And I knew the secrets in your spires  
And I knew the emptiness of youth  
And I knew the solitude of hearts  
And I knew the murmurs of the soul  
And I knew the silence of the world"  
  
[Debra - Beck
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1004548%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.bBFjHQ)  
This song is so funny. Firstly, the music is awesome, old style R &B, totally
over the top, but smooth and sexy. Add on top of that ridiculous lyrics about
meeting a girl at JC Penny (a clothing store) and you have a recipe for
classic Beck.  
  
[Son of a Preacher Man - Dusty Springfield
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3518242%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.msrVz6)  
A great soul song about a woman being in love with with the preacher's son and
the excitement that comes from the sin of forbidden fruit. Terrific music and
backup vocals, too.  
  
[Girl, You'll Be a Woman Soon - Urge Overkill
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3518245%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.iF2nP0)  
Song about a man who's in love with a girl, but her parents think he's no
good. Sexy sexy song.  
  
[All My Little Words - The Magnetic Fields
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1124841%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.UQ1EUI)  
A pretty little love song with phrases like "not for all the tea in China" and
new words like "un-boyfriendable"  
  
[The Luckiest Guy on the Lower East Side - The Magnetic Fields
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1124846%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.UcwliF)  
Cute love song about a guy who's the luckiest on the lower east side because
he has wheels (means he has a car) and the girl he likes wants to go for a
ride.  
  
[Distraction #74 - The Avett Brothers
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2490405%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.ThZ527)  
This self-deprecating (self-criticizing) song is about a guy who "kind of
loved two girls and then he kind of lost them both". There's some really fun
interplay between the two singers who exchange words in rapid succession.  
  
[Leaving On A Jet Plane - Peter, Paul & Mary
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768923453%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.NAcgYA)  
One of the few love songs that makes it onto my list. I'm not a sentimental
person, but this beautiful song about a man who's saying goodbye to his
girlfriend touches me every time I hear it.  
  
[If I Loved You - Carousel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773010476%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.qE6z03)  
From the musical Carousel, one of the most interesting love songs. Instead of
the two protagonists directly professing their love for each other, the love
at the center of this song is hypothetical, with that conditional preposition
making all the difference " _If_ I loved you".  
  
[Tonight - West Side Story
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770011573%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.MfBihC)  
From the musical West Side Story, this song is first sung as a duet between
the star-crossed lovers Tony and Maria (modeled after Romeo and Juliet). When
later the entire cast joins the song, with Sharks and the Jets turning it into
a violent, macho prelude to the rumble, it brings down the house in one of the
greatest staged company numbers in Broadway history.  
  
[Somewhere - West Side Story
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2081344%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.AiGL6Z)  
The most haunting song in West Side Story, wherein the young lovers search for
a place where their love can be accepted.  
  
[A Little Fall of Rain - Les Miserables
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769424210%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.gpAsV1)  
*spoiler alter*  
As Eponine dies in his hands, Maurius tries to comfort her.  
  
 **Motivational Songs - 励志性歌曲**  
  
[Move on Up - Curtis Mayfield
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1477181%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.YEaelt)  
This song is amazing musically. The lyrics are also not bad, very
motivational, encouraging those who are down and out to stand up strong and
improve themselves.  
  
[My Culture - 1 Giant Leap
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2539788%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.jQw8eB)  
This little-known jazz-rap group has some great music. This song is about how
we come from a long line of ancestors and how it is important to treasure and
value the culture that we have inherited from them.  
  
[Friends - Bette Midler
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3324404%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.AIKPVa)  
A moving song about a woman who doesn't have many friends, but makes some new
friends. Sounds simple, but it's a great song from one of the greatest
crooners in history.  
  
[I Will Survive - Gloria Gaynor
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1406309%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.IBbJlE)  
This is one of the great disco and dance anthems of all time. The lyrics are
simple, but powerful, about how women should be strong and not rely on a man,
and when they face hardship or break up with their boyfriends, it's not the
end of the world, they will survive. Terrific, catchy song, one of my all-time
favorites.  
  
[Hold My Hand - Hootie & the Blowfish
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1040247%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.yj8YcU)  
This song was on the first CD I ever owned. It's a fabulous, catchy song that
makes you want to sing along. The lyrics are easy to learn, and the message is
clear and uplifting. If you're in trouble, don't worry, I'll help you, just
hold my hand"  
  
[One - U2
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1104803%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.PFZwi2)  
This is one of U2's greatest songs. The lyrics are simplistic but packed with
meaning. This song is about universal love, peace, and humanity.  
  
[Drift Away - Dobie Gray
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769109169%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.JJTKzT)  
A feel-good song about the great feeling we can get just by listening to some
good music. "Give me the beat boys to free my soul, I wanna get lost in your
rock n roll and drift away".  
  
[You'll Never Walk Alone - Carousel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1773010469%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.pChloG)  
In this excellent musical, the antihero Billy has died a tragic death, and
this song is sung to his widowed wife Laurie to encourage her not to give up.
In the end, when Laurie's own daughter is grown up and feeling helpless and
lost, Billy comes back as a ghost and sings this song to her to give her
strength.  
  
[Let The Sun Shine - Hair
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1769243287%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.12.mst8ij)  
This song takes place at the end of the protest rock musical Hair. The
protagonist has been shipped off to the Vietnam War, but the musical ends on a
hopeful note that if enough people want peace, peace can be achieved, and we
can "let the sun shine in".  
  
[Something's Coming - West Side Story
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770011569%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.13.4PxQDK)  
Tony sings this song early in the musical West Side Story describing a
premonition he has that something is going to happen. Sure enough, that night
he meets and falls in love with Maria. Gorgeous, earnest song and hopeful
lyrics.  
  
[Climb Every Mountain - The Sound of Music
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1770355111%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.1.PrU32y)  
Mother Abbess sings this song to Maria when she has given up, in order to
encourage her to face her fears and live her life. In the finale, as the von
Trapps escape to Switzerland, it is sung once again to encourage them in their
flight from the Nazis.  
  
 **Nostalgic Songs - 怀旧歌曲**  
  
[In My Life - The Beatles
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1003882%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.FRQipN)  
One of the Beatles' best, about looking back on one's childhood places.  
  
[The River - Bruce Springsteen
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1292883%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.v217UQ)  
Bruce Springsteen sings about blue collar working class life in America's Rust
Belt. This song is about reminiscing about youthful love and loss.  
  
[Homeward Bound - Simon & Garfunkel
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1283250%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.14.nzmh9x)  
This song is about being on the road performing all the time and missing home.  
  
[My Hometown - Bruce Springsteen
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1292978%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.8c5x3x)  
The lyrics in this rock song are packed with emotion and meaning and social
commentary, about a rust belt town in American which has fallen on hard times.  
  
[American Pie - Don McLean
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/3368866%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.YfeDHw)  
Most of you have probably heard this song. It's one of my all-time favorites.
Don McLean is singing about the first two decades in the history of rock n
roll music (the 1950s and the 1960s). The song is full of symbolism. The
"Joker" is Bob Dylan. The "Quartet" is the Beatles. The "girl who sang the
blues" is Janis Joplin. The "Day the music died" is the day the plane carrying
Buddy Holly crashed killing him. Don McLean is singing about his love of rock
music, and in turn he created a classic rock song himself.  
  
[Acres of Corn - Iris Dement
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/2764603%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.mZ6A7N)  
This song is sung by a woman who immigrated from Ireland to a farm in 19th
century United States. She once had dreams of going to Paris, but now she's a
farmer's wife and the only thing she has to look forward to is the acres of
corn outside her farm. Beautiful song.  
  
[Ode to My Family - The Cranberries
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1767420%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.2.wURUlz)  
This beautiful song by the Cranberries is about how when you're little you
think the world is such a happy and good place, and then you grow up and find
it's harder than you realized, but she still loves her family and remembers
the good childhood they gave her.  
  
[Gus: The Theatre - Cats
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.xiami.com/song/1768932289%3Fspm%3Da1z1s.3521865.23309997.12.UkA1Wc)  
Cats is a musical about....cats. In this musical, cats can talk and sing and
have jobs, like train attendant and magician. This song is about a cat who was
an actor, but now he is very old. It's a very touching song about a cat who
doesn't want to give up his pride, even though he is approaching old age.


## [如何评价周杰伦的《乱舞春秋》？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/34526375/answer/149805441)
谢邀

《乱舞春秋》是一首中国风嘻哈作品，是具有开创性的Chinese Hip-Hop。

《乱舞春秋》在周杰伦众多歌迷中奉为神作，可我没想到，它也是如此冷门的一部作品。关于《乱舞春秋》，网上能查阅到的资料不多，乐评也几乎没有。

《乱舞春秋》是周杰伦最为复杂的作品之一，是周杰伦代表高度的中国风西化革命性作品之一，是周杰伦最为狂妄的作品之一。

甚至，某些方面来说，没有之一。

周杰伦、方文山、钟兴民，我只能跪着感谢那个时代下这三位， **狂 妄的创作者**。

![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-40f6f55f03e405f607199876b14ff773_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1024'%20height='448'></svg>)  

首先，来看一下《乱舞春秋》的制作阵容：

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-1a3da494c6facf4867ef4004f28c856c_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='2314'%20height='1094'></svg>)

07 乱舞春秋

 **制 作人：周杰伦 词：方文山 曲：周杰伦 编曲：钟兴民 ** 和声：周杰伦 和声编写：周杰伦 吉他：黄中岳 鼓：陈柏州 Scratch：陈正男
录音工程：柯宗佑（Alfa Studio） 混音工程：杨大纬（杨大纬录音工作室）

《乱舞春秋》 是网络游戏《乱舞三国》的主题曲 。

==========================================

在谈这首歌前必须先说的一些历史，不然讲不清这首歌

==========================================

周杰伦一直给人的态度就是：狂拽酷炫叼。那么你们认为周杰伦最狂的时期在什么时候？你觉得周杰伦真正玩到脱的专辑是哪一张？《惊叹号》？

 **错 ，正是这张专辑《七里香》。**

《七里香》是《叶惠美》的延续，前前一张专辑《八度空间》0奖项，刺激了周杰伦，所以他在《叶惠美》（许多杰米眼中的周杰伦排名第一的专辑）中，他做出了重大的突破，从任何方面都提高了水平。2004年05月08日的第15届金曲奖上，周杰伦从罗大佑和舒淇手中斩获年度最高荣誉：最佳华语流行专辑奖。一个出道了仅仅4年，发行了4张专辑的音乐人。3张就获得了金曲奖的最高奖项。那时年轻气盛的周，不可一世，才华横溢。

2004年08月03日，《七里香》发行，这是周杰伦第一次用歌曲名命名专辑。

2004年，对于周杰伦来说，还有更大的一个关键点是：他开始进入了大陆音乐的主流。2004年春晚，周杰伦第一次登上中央春节晚会。演唱一首绝对冷门风格的曲目《龙拳》。

[2004年春晚 音乐《龙拳》演唱：周杰伦 2004年春晚_2004年春晚_视频_央视网
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//tv.cntv.cn/video/C13406/3391d508456242149144262f5d908848)

在
周杰伦之前，没有人用这样的曲风，站在主流的舞台上。2004年，到处都在响彻《七里香》这首歌，无论是校园里，还是大街上。《我的地盘》陪着动感地带唱片店CD店里《七里香》专辑被抢购一空，很多人想要买到，还得排队等订货。2004年，随着《无与伦比》演唱会，周杰伦开始诞生一个词伴随着他：
**" 无与伦比"。**

 **我 想，这是只有经历过那一年的人们，才会体会到的周氏风暴。**

  

 **好 了，那么重点来了。**

  

 **许 多人都说：嘻哈、摇滚什么的在中国是小众，火不起来的。中国只有pop口水慢歌能火。**

 **有 些自视清高的听众说：周杰伦只会唱些情情爱爱的校园风歌曲，毫无营养毫无灵魂毫无深度毫无技术毫无内涵毫无意义……**

  
![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-afffd0628f55f114e68342ce6c2f6e87_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='512'%20height='348'></svg>)  

好，既然你们说情情爱爱是芭乐音乐，那我就把所有情爱的音乐都归为芭乐口水歌。我姑且就算有关爱情的音乐就是垃圾就是芭乐口水歌。

那么请看《七里香》的专辑曲目：

1.我的地盘

2.七里香

3.借口

4.外婆

5.将军

6.搁浅

7.乱舞春秋

8.困兽之斗

9.游园会

10.止战之殇

 **这 十首歌中只有《七里香》《借口》《搁浅》《园游会》4首歌是情爱歌曲。**

 **曲 风包括Hip-Hop、摇滚、中国风、POP、R&B等等。**

 **歌 曲涉及青春、亲情、反战、自由、挣扎、历史、国粹等等。**

![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-fe9f4689e1f57c26cf417977dad72bb1_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='800'%20height='400'></svg>)

我一直在自己的回答说，形容周杰伦最贴切的词，是狂妄。因为狂妄，是一种来着于他本人内心的本质情怀，也是实现在他作品上的绝对水平。

《乱舞春秋》，正是那个时期周杰伦狂妄的团队里。

 **最 为狂妄的周杰伦。作曲。**

 **最 为狂妄的方文山。作词。**

 **最 为狂妄的钟兴民。编曲。**

  

==========================================

从词编曲上，解析《乱舞春秋》神在哪里

=========================================

先从词开始，我把从网上找的谱一同贴上：

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-71f5323cdbb860300acdee2089a06794_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='768'%20height='1088'></svg>)

《 乱舞春秋 》虽然在听众的眼里是冷门歌曲，但是，在专业领域，他可不冷门。

 **《 乱舞春秋》的歌词，可是被用于写专业文学论文的！**

  
![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-c7584ad10e0f4280ce678c99eacec4d8_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='416'%20height='686'></svg>)

《乱舞春秋》描写的是一个现代少年通过时光机穿越回到古代的三国时期的所见所闻及他对三国时期的理解。

三国，无疑是中国历史上最迷人的时代。无论是《三国志》、《三国演绎》还是数不胜数的三国衍生产品比如游戏、歌曲、音乐、绘画等，都数不胜数。那是个英雄美人谋士名将辈出，引领一时风骚；阴谋策略阵仗杀戮，苦此生民的充满戏剧性及故事性的时代。

而方文山，用短短四百字的歌词，描绘出了一个新奇的角度、一个全新的角度、一个天马行空的角度去看待这一段历史。

"那混乱年代，朝廷太腐败……读三国历史的兴衰 想去瞧个明白"：通过交代动机的同时，将三国的背景描绘了。

"看看看就马上回来 ……"中二少年充满好奇地做上时光机，好像哆啦A梦一样，像童话一样穿越到古代去了……66666

"江山，我站在云端……五官差点离开身体，还好有时光机我谢谢你"有趣吧，一个少年飞来飞去，既身临其境又置身事外，看着世间的纷争。

"曹魏枭雄在，蜀汉多人才，东吴将士怪，七星连环败，诸葛亮的天命不来……"这些书都有记载，不是文山兄在乱掰。那些历史上恢弘的故事，那些精彩的片段，在方文山笔下就是写得这么逗趣好玩，漫不经心地就写道了三国。而整首曲子的调性，就是那一句：

 **" 我呸，谁也不服谁，我是龟你是鳖 "啦啦啦啦……**

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-f8b12f3b336108b1ed84f22a4bb6b5c2_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='300'%20height='317'></svg>)

这就是一个狂妄的少年，天马行空地看待三国的故事。而这个故事来自于34岁的： **方 文山。**

 **这 首歌，光是看这个歌词，就已经是一个了不起的作品。他丝毫不亚于周杰伦的曲，一样的天马行空，一样的角度新颖，一样的与众不同。**

  

=======================

然后是编曲部分，钟兴民大师

=======================

《乱舞春秋》的编曲，让人不得不佩服钟兴民不愧是华语乐团的大师。

众所周知，钟兴民给人的印象是他是一个学院派的弦乐大场面大神。但是，大家很少注意到，钟兴民的编曲风格涉猎非常广，比如在《乱舞春秋》中，他做了看上去应该是洪敬尧、林迈可的"活"：打碟HipHop、电子游戏音效。延续了上一张专辑中《双刀》的风格。

[如何评价周杰伦的《双刀》? - 元吉的回答 \-
知乎](https://www.zhihu.com/question/41568565/answer/145992906)

乱舞春秋一开场，便用万马奔腾和马的嘶鸣声拉开了帷幕。这是一个充满战争的乱世时期。画面感极强。

然后吉他扫弦，鼓点加入。OK，现代流行音乐。在《乱舞春秋》中，最为出彩的是钟兴民大师选择了一个极其具有辨析度的鼓，
特别是低音鼓点，非常有力度，听起来非常爽！

然后，神tm的……电子游戏里的人物音效进来了！有人分析这是《街霸2》里春丽挑衅的声音。好吧，把电子游戏融合到编曲中来，和方文山的词完美契合：这真的是一个在打电玩的中二少年的奇妙之旅。

然后，嘻哈音乐的打碟也进来了！哈哈~这样的一首彻头彻尾的嘻哈音乐，怎么能缺了打碟呢！爽~

然后，间奏来了！佩服啊佩服啊！ **间 奏的琵琶搭配擦碟再加电子游戏人声！**

![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-9372e90f262f9520d50155371ea05e25_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='693'%20height='34'></svg>)

我在这一段旋律出来的时候！真心给跪了啊。

 **但 是！一切都没有这个地方神TM：**

  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-128695bcc56f7aec130042810389e6ee_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='577'%20height='182'></svg>)  
![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-f20a953b21ae6adba5349993c23bc029_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='800'%20height='400'></svg>)

简直了好么！谁tm会在一段音乐中加这种有的没得环节。钟兴民老师在这里想起了手机铃声，我tm无数次以为是不是我手机响了？然后通话时的信号干扰声……简直太传神了！

给跪了！

 **我 想做出这一段时，周杰伦应该和钟兴民都在一旁，被自己逗得笑得合不拢嘴吧。**

 **然
后到了最后，人声唱完，几个超级爽的重鼓点出来，然后鼓点+打碟+电子游戏人声音效全部融合在一起甩出来。气势磅礴，这是钟兴民独有的炫技大招！大招！大招！所有的音效在这时奔腾翻滚，一方面迎合了三国乱世的主题，一方面极具画面感的总结了这个中二少年的奇幻穿越时空之旅。**
**最 后五声大笑就这样把三国给笑的没脾气了…… 完美！佩服！**

 **真 正的大师，一方面创新出别人不敢想，一方面做到别人做不到：钟兴民是也。**

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-c6cc0e704f4c8b478f5704b3c0986dde_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='550'%20height='823'></svg>)

============================================

最后，解析《乱舞春秋》神曲所在：极尽炫技8段落作曲

============================================

你们应该知道了，《乱舞春秋》周杰伦写了8个段落。

8个段落……8个段落啊！！！！！

先解释一下，大多数歌曲，段落基本是ABAB，就是主歌副歌然后再重复一遍，结束了。

好一些的：就是ABCB或者B'，然后结束。

再好一些的，能在段落中呈现"起承转合"的意境。这种音乐已经是流行歌曲中凤毛麟角的佳作了……

而乱舞春秋呢……

ABCDEFGHEE'E''……起、承、新起、转、再转、再再转、……

![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-c162612e6ccd10e809cdbed248eac767_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='200'%20height='200'></svg>)  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-686e582e225e3ddc12d886baa4a81a72_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='324'%20height='273'></svg>)  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-be63a36c1a4f7017bf58dca509a8cdc2_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='500'%20height='265'></svg>)

 **炫 技也不带这样玩的！炫技也不带这样玩的！**

  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-8bbc885bd99cd28c747da923ceea903e_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='800'%20height='400'></svg>)

然后，在这首歌里边，周杰伦在第一次主歌里，就运用了3次转调技术！

全曲他还运用了至少3个不同的唱腔。

  

 **还 是先给大家列一下段落：**

A："那混乱的年代……想去瞧个明白"

B："刀剑棍棒……老实说有点紧张"

C："江山，我站在云端 ……在兵荒马乱"

D："望着天眼看……我是龟你是鳖啦啦啦……"

 **E ："妖兽扰乱人间次序……好有时光机我谢谢你"（副歌）**

 **F ：" 曹魏枭雄在 ……等到东方鱼肚白我再来跟你说High"**

 **G ：" 嘴里有刀 …… 转身忘掉 "**

 **H ：" 黄巾贼你不要吵倭 …… 去找皇帝老爷讨 "**

  

 **请 大家一定切记EFGH这四个段落的加粗重点标注。**

  

首先，是第一遍的主歌。A；

然后一个酷炫的36分3连音"看看看"就马上回来，转到段落B；

然后"啊啊"两声（估计周杰伦临时乱加的）， **曲 子在这时转调了！进入了段落C；**

  

 **绝 大多数的歌曲，在这个段落之后，就应该进入副歌了！**

 **然 而，《乱舞春秋》在这里搞了一个巨大的转折，C段结束** **后 ！又转调！升半音后进入段落D；**

  

 **迎 来《乱舞春秋》里最为妖娆的一个经典段落。**

![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-261b0df6d4263bb71b297af2b46c48bb_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='377'%20height='53'></svg>)

然后进入副歌，段落E；

一段超赞的琵琶+打碟+电子游戏人声音效的间奏后，接上段落F；

F后转到G

 **然 后！重点来了！**

 **和 声！周氏最具招牌的"复调"来了！**

 **在 H进来的时候！G依然在着，G和H本来就是两段完全不同的旋律，而在这里就构成了和声，"复调"的表现形式。**

然后G消失，H独自重复一遍。

然后接入副歌重复E。

然后又一次间奏，再次重复副歌E。

然后经典的"订外卖片段"，副歌E片段改变声调后最为背景乐E'

 **然 后一个静音之后！E'依然作为背景底乐，G提高了八度变为G'加进来！在这里，G和E两个完全不同的旋律段落又构成了"复调"形式的和声。**

 **最 后，在一段钟兴民大师酷炫的炫技，万马奔腾+打碟+游戏音效后，结束。**

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-166445aa8d4e2fad7bf96e338c8997fa_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='690'%20height='690'></svg>)

周杰伦写一首歌，几乎够别人作一张专辑了。跪在地上的我，至今不能释怀。

![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-bbec061173eb435b9ce4cacfff99bff9_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='337'%20height='271'></svg>)  

 **=========================**

 **总 结**

 **=========================**

 **《 乱舞春秋》**
是周杰伦独树一帜的"中国风"歌曲，这首歌曲体现了周杰伦对传统文化的牢固把握，对中国元素的坚持运用，并用时尚的国外西方音乐手法表现中国古典情怀的经典作品。

在这首歌中，无论是词曲编录混，都是真正完美的。全10分的存在。周杰伦的曲、方文山的词、钟兴民的编，都是他们用最为狂妄的炫技来展现自己的才华于实力的地方。这是一个炫到令人发指的高度。

而更可怕的是，在2004年的《七里香》这张专辑中，除了《乱舞春秋》，还有《止战之殇》、《将军》、《我的地盘》、《外婆》、《七里香》、《搁浅》这样的又是满是干货的顶级作品。

我想起邓柯在今年《歌手》的乐评中，对迪玛希的实力这样描述：

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-e62361f87427f62e474018ea6d0de30a_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='619'%20height='79'></svg>)  

[如何评价迪玛希的唱功？ \- 邓柯的回答 \-
知乎](https://www.zhihu.com/question/55007794/answer/142246722)

  

 **借 此引用一下：在那个周杰伦最为才华爆棚的时期，当他和其它歌手站在100米决赛跑道上。他的实力足够在别人跑到终点前，他自己先跑个往返----
跑到终点后跑回起点拿起手机，然后再向终点冲刺。在即将超越所有对手的时候，他感到肚子饿了，于是接通手机定了份外卖鸡排饭。**

 **并 叮嘱好，我还要加个蛋。**


## [如何评价老狼的音乐？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/22334293/answer/91832924)
**千 呼万唤，老狼终于登上了《我是歌手》。亮相前的短片里，老搭档高晓松录制了一段视频，评价老狼是"不管在多么喧嚣的时代，都能安静唱歌的典范"。**

  

 **全 场灯光点亮，老狼一袭黑色长风衣，双手握着立式话筒，唱完了朴树的《旅途》。**

  

 **当 "** **我 们路过高山，** **我 们路过湖泊，** **我 们路过森林，** **路 过沙漠，** **路 过人们的城堡和花园。**
**" 的副歌响起，仿佛命运的长河开始流淌，时间的隧道缓缓开启。**

 **仅 仅几个小时之前，许巍正式发表高晓松包办词曲的新歌《生活不止眼前的苟且》。** **当
高晓松写下"生活不止眼前的苟且，还有诗和远方的田野。你赤手空拳来到人世间，为找到那片海不顾一切"，恰似一个轮回，时针拨过20年。**

  

 **偶
尔怀恋起过去，念旧的人会说："我的故乡，在80年代"。那时候有青青草地，有皓月繁星，有睡在我上铺的兄弟和同桌的你。那时候天总是很蓝，日子总过得太慢，文学、爱情和穿越世界的旅行，是萦绕良久的话题。**

  

 **校 园里的男生常常抱着吉他，女生围坐在旁边，痴痴地听。白衣飘飘，是抹不去的青春印记。自由的歌者，像是天地间的盖世英雄。**

  
![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/bd178033ce36cacc3cff21ad50bbebb9_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='900'%20height='600'></svg>)  

 **当 时，一支叫"青铜器"的大学生摇滚乐队，在不少地下演出中，与崔健、唐朝、黑豹同台。老狼和高晓松，都是乐队成员。**

  

 **1990
年的暑假，老狼和高晓松收到海南一家歌厅的驻唱邀请，返程时因路费不足，到厦门停留大半年。《同桌的你》《白衣飘飘的年代》《青春无悔》等传唱多时的作品，得以完成初稿。**

  

 **如 今想来，一次横跨南北的远行，几首形同朦胧诗的歌词，数段质朴而亲切的旋律，几乎是强烈的暗示：校园民谣此后的深刻印记，脱胎于对诗和远方的原始憧憬。**
**而 如果没有老狼，诗和远方根本无从谈起。**

  
![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/9317ec5d11b1e978c040c5c82d94b690_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='400'%20height='265'></svg>)  

 **和 高晓松一样，老狼出生于高知家庭，父亲是航空航天的总工，母亲则是中央广播交响乐团团长。大学主修无线电的他，也走上了音乐道路。**

  

 **1994
年，大地唱片发行了影响深远的专辑《校园民谣1》，已在乐坛滚打数年的老狼，演唱了高晓松填词谱曲的三首作品：《同桌的你》《睡在我上铺的兄弟》《流浪歌手的情人》。专辑最终实现了近60万张的销量。**

  

 **老 狼清亮中带点沧桑的声线，唱尽了校园的天然与美好。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/93743060/w0172d7tzx2_160_90_3.jpg)
《睡在我上铺的兄弟》老狼 现场版 http://v.qq.com/boke/page/w/0/2/w0172d7tzx2.html
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/boke/page/w/0/2/w0172d7tzx2.html)**

  

**《
睡在我上铺的兄弟》，源自高晓松在酒桌上接到的一个电话。睡在上铺的兄弟，毕业后各奔东西，远方的问候，调动了往日的思绪。沉吟一小时之后，便有了这样的字句：**

  

> 你来的信写的越来越客气，关于爱情你只字不提

>

> 你说你现在有很多的朋友，却再也不为那些事忧愁

>

> 分给我烟抽的兄弟，分给我快乐的往昔

>

> 你曾经问我的那些问题，如今再没人问起

 **今 昔恍惚，理想与现实之间的沟壑，成为校园民谣歌咏的主题。**

  

 **同
一年，老狼参加中央电视台"94大学生毕业晚会"。在这台云集了何炅、杨澜、姜丰等人的晚会上，老狼唱起《同桌的你》，并将这首歌催生的感动，延续到第二年的春晚舞台。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/32676784/y0126zogzsq_160_90_3.jpg) 老狼-
同桌的你MV_标清 http://v.qq.com/boke/page/y/0/q/y0126zogzsq.html
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/boke/page/y/0/q/y0126zogzsq.html)  
**

**据
说，《同桌的你》是高晓松在为初恋女友梳理头发时迸发的灵感。"谁娶了多愁善感的你，谁看了你的日记，谁把你的长发盘起，谁把你的长发盘起，谁给你做的嫁衣"，并没有错失所爱的痛苦，取而代之的是轻微的怅然与由衷的祝福。**  

  

 **日
记、相片、半块橡皮，最寻常的物件，寄寓了一时的深情。爱哭的你嫁作人妇，"我也将有我的妻"，谁看了我给你写的信，谁把它丢在风里。纵然遗憾，却哀而不伤。某种程度上，这也是校园民谣共同的基调。**

  

 **1995
年初，大红大紫的老狼推出首张个人专辑《恋恋风尘》，发行20天就创下23万张的销售纪录，成为当年的内地票房冠军。此时的老狼，已开始试图挣脱"校园民谣"的标签，诠释更纯粹的爱情主题。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/22573862/j00191maqnt_160_90_3.jpg)
高晓松、老狼《恋恋风尘》Live http://v.qq.com/cover/t/tbrn2ajco5izb0g.html?vid=j00191maqnt
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/cover/t/tbrn2ajco5izb0g.html%3Fvid%3Dj00191maqnt)**

  

**同
名主打歌提到黄昏的白雪，开满山岗的忧伤，女孩带着我的恋歌，在朝霞里迎风吟唱。"露水挂在发梢，结满透明的惆怅，是我一生最初的迷惘"之类的歌词，已经形同诗歌，"相信爱的年纪，没能唱给你的歌曲，让我一生中常常追忆"，又是熟悉的凭吊。**

  

 **在 我心目中，老狼最好听的歌曲，并不是《同桌的你》，而是《青春无悔》。在高晓松1996年出版的同名作品集里，老狼和叶蓓一起，唱着普世的青春情愫。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/90833546/l0013l4wmf0_160_90_3.jpg) 青春无悔
(feat. 叶蓓) [2014湖北卫视春晚 Live]
http://v.qq.com/cover/p/p2m642rkxe45c4p.html?vid=l0013l4wmf0
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/cover/p/p2m642rkxe45c4p.html%3Fvid%3Dl0013l4wmf0)**

  

**"
你说你青春无悔包括对我的爱恋，你说岁月会改变相许终生的誓言，你说亲爱的道声再见，转过年轻的脸，含笑的带泪的不变的眼。"多少人说过同样的话，做过同样的事，经历过同样的离别，最后又收归在同样的"青春"的名义下，变成最幽微的心事。**  

  

 **《 青春无悔》里，老狼还有两首动人的歌。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/16263070/g0013e6f91h_160_90_3.jpg) 高晓松老狼
模范情书官方正版MV http://v.qq.com/page/g/0/h/g0013e6f91h.html
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/page/g/0/h/g0013e6f91h.html)**

  

**《
模范情书》开篇，轻巧的旋律，对应四句比喻连排，"我是你闲坐窗前的那棵橡树，我是你初次流泪时手边的书，我是你春夜注视的那段蜡烛，我是你秋天穿上的楚楚衣服。"**

  

 **若
是春夜和蜡烛关联"春蚕到死丝方尽，蜡炬成灰泪始干"还不够确凿，以橡树自比，完全是颇具年代感的表述。舒婷的《致橡树》，确立男性稳重可靠的标准："伟岸的身躯"和"坚持的位置"。**

  

 **可 《模范情书》最后两句："我像每个恋爱的孩子一样，在大街上琴弦上寂寞成长。"又成功消解了庄严，以烂漫和青涩调和。由老狼来演唱，再合适不过。**

  

[ ![](http://r3.ykimg.com/0542020852C82E226A0A4A56F55A9AD6) 老狼演唱会小柯伴奏久违的事
小柯即兴演唱夕阳往事因为爱情--在线播放--优酷网，视频高清在线观看
http://v.youku.com/v_show/id_XMzk5MzQzODg0.html?from=s1.8-1-1.2
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.youku.com/v_show/id_XMzk5MzQzODg0.html%3Ffrom%3Ds1.8-1-1.2)

  

**《
久违的事》，也满载那段时光里的含蓄。"久违的事想起还是甜的，久违的人你还在相册的第一篇，你留下的蓝信箱我不时还要看一看，你带走的粉窗帘如今飘在谁窗前。"**  

  

 **当
对岸更成熟更商业的流行乐坛在渲染"对你爱爱爱不完"的直接，在地的情歌却着力雕琢细节里的触动："岁月不留痕忘了相亲相爱的人，你我也会苍老连相片也看不清，只有你的小东西还藏在我的日记本里，红的像火一片枫叶上面刻着你和我的心。"**

  

 **现 在，还有谁会用刻下心型的枫叶来见证彼此的情意。那份郑重，随着歌声飘散风里，化身历史仅有的证据。**

  

 **[![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/68218149/o001380s9h6_160_90_3.jpg) 晴朗(live版)
http://v.qq.com/page/o/0/6/o001380s9h6.html
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/page/o/0/6/o001380s9h6.html)**

  

**老
狼并不是一位高产的歌者。直到2002年，他才推出第二张个人专辑《晴朗》。这张专辑里最著名的歌，或许是经由去年的《中国好声音》，重新回到公众视野的《虎口脱险》。**

  

 **彼
时在校园里放声歌唱的朋友们，比如高晓松，比如郁冬，仍旧和老狼站在一起。但配器从吉他走向钢琴和弦乐，甚至有电子乐器出现，也足见老狼求变的决心。许巍作词作曲的《晴朗》，也灌注了此前并不属于老狼的元素。**

  

 **我
时常会想，在今天这个视改编为政治正确、以创新做绝佳卖点的时代，应该如何回望曾经的校园民谣。老狼和高晓松们，又会怎样看待当初的自己。是懊悔少作的稚嫩，还是怀念旧日的纯真？是牵动珍藏的记忆，还是感恩生命的馈赠？**

  

 **至
少，不容抹灭的事实是，他们替流行音乐留下了重要的向度，也为大众心灵呼喊着诗和远方。校园是一个终将醒来的梦，但有梦的欢愉，总胜过无梦的干枯。那些吟咏歌唱的人，都是我们的造梦师。**

  

 **2007 年，专辑《北京的冬天》面世。从人心到地理，老狼的意图有所递迁。但一首《想把我唱给你听》，可能是一路走来的绝佳自况：**

  

[ ![](http://vpic.video.qq.com/93498628/j0016jylcsn_160_90_3.jpg) 老狼
王婧《想把我唱给你听 》 http://v.qq.com/page/j/0/n/j0016jylcsn.html
](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//v.qq.com/page/j/0/n/j0016jylcsn.html)

  

> 想把我唱给你听，趁现在年少如花

>

> 花儿尽情地开吧，装点你的岁月我的枝芽

>

> 谁能够代替你呢，趁年轻尽情地爱吧

>

> 最最亲爱的人啊，路途遥远我们在一起吧

  

 **人 都要老的，幸好青春是一首不老的歌。**


## [选秀节目中为什么很少人翻唱周杰伦的歌?](https://www.zhihu.com/question/21402380/answer/53390360)
写歌的人最懂歌，以及有些歌真的只有他能唱，甚至与唱功无关，只有他才能唱出歌词所表达的感觉。  
  
我记得《十一月的肖邦》发行的时候，有乐评人提到《珊瑚海》这首歌唱得差，不该跟梁心颐合唱，因为一对比把周杰伦声线和唱功的缺点全部展露无遗，这个评价留在我的脑海里很多年，以至于我此后每次听这首歌都会去注意是否真的唱得那么差，但是这么多年过去了，听了无数对唱的版本，发现只有周杰伦才能唱出"海鸟跟鱼相爱，只是一场意外"那种无奈的悲伤。  
  
《以父之名》应该是很多杰迷的最爱之一，不知道有多少男生学唱过这首歌，请你们告诉我第一句"微凉的晨露沾湿黑礼服
石板路有雾父在低诉"，怎么找调？！还有找到调后怎么唱出那种不可一世却又肩负责任的教父感？  
  
林志炫在我是歌手唱过《烟花易冷》，唱功真的太扎实，声线太优美！可是不感人，怎么听都不感人，杰伦的《烟花易冷》声音沙沙的，淡淡的，听完后会让人有一种堕入空门的冲动，那句"雨纷纷
旧故里草木深 我听闻 你始终一个人"低吟浅唱，不知道让多少人潸然泪下。  
  
还有《七里香》，这首歌有多好听我都不需要赘述了，之前有人在微博问你最爱周杰伦的哪一首歌？接近上万答案，翻评论差不多一半都是《七里香》。我想说的是请仔细听那句"那饱满的稻穗
幸福了这个季节
而你的脸颊像田里熟透的蕃茄"，他的发音，吐词，感情投入简直如一支神笔完美地呈现了歌词表达的画面，会让人想象杰伦似乎在唱的时候也露出了他招牌式的害羞低头微笑，然后听歌的自己也跟着害羞地低头，脸成了红番茄。你说，这还怎么翻唱！  
  
不得不说我的最爱《开不了口》，嘘，别说话，用心感受那句"安静地听你撒娇 看你睡着一直到老"，真是恨不得让时间就在这一刻地老天荒。  
  
栗子太多，就不一一举了。。。  
所以有如此经典的演绎，选秀歌手还怎么唱？借用一下楼上
[@修名瓷](https://www.zhihu.com/people/bd13bd67561b7ea07bda5a3be96c7501) 的最后一句话：  
唱！功！多！好！的！来！翻！唱！也！不！如！周！董！的！听！着！舒！服！


## [五月天究竟是不是台独？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/63054283/answer/214620538)
![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-b8d28e84919dc396f846a2ea60f56e5d_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1080'%20height='1076'></svg>)

  

上面是最初的问题，还好我保留了截图，题主被迫修改问题，表示理解，毕竟我也被迫修改了回答，"五月天是台独"怎么就"政治敏感"了呢？至今也不明白。

大家可以查看一下这个问题的日志，某些人为了不让别人讨论五月天是不是台独，可以恶意编辑，把原来的题目改的面目全非，这不是 **欲 盖弥彰**吗？

图片部分来自网络，侵删。

多图预警！  

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-275f6261f294dde9b88dd5a700add3b4_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1080'%20height='1732'></svg>)![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-5c7d56b310547e4d6a985af7ec5a9f2f_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1080'%20height='1252'></svg>)

  

##  先上结论： **五 月天是台独**。

这里说的台独指的是参与台独活动和支持台独立场的台独分子。

且听我一一证明。

①五月天1996年未成军前在" **台 湾要建国**"晚会演出，当时乐队的名字还叫做SO
BAND，1997年才改名叫做"五月天"。阿信卖力演唱《母亲ヘ名叫台湾》等歌，这首歌是被很多台独分子奉为"台湾国歌"的。这个晚会看名字就知道是个台独集会活动，五月天总不能说事先不知道。此处给出当时的视频链接[https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xt_jEQW_xDM
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.youtube.com/watch%3Fv%3Dxt_jEQW_xDM)

不 方面上外网的，可以看这个[https://pan.baidu.com/s/1eSONEvS
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//pan.baidu.com/s/1eSONEvS)

在 此，特别感谢台湾网友
[@路人甲](https://www.zhihu.com/people/ebaecee02dc4a84a5ccb7569eb6f69e0)
提供的图片和视频，反台独永远不能少了台湾同胞！

  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-f6e7d0b1eddc66efa68ed2b1e9e1ddc2_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='480'%20height='360'></svg>)![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-df2849c9067fab0c452fdc1e7b568b28_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='120'%20height='80'></svg>)

有大陆歌迷疑惑，为什么从没听过五月天唱过爱国歌曲。得到的回答是五月天是什么"世界公民"，不蓝不绿也不红，更强调大爱，像什么《这个世界》《晚安地球人》。我听了很伤感，傻孩子，人家当然爱国，只不过
**爱 的和你不是同一国**罢了。  

②据《TVBS周刊》报道，五月天阿信是 **民
进党员**，在学生时代即加入民进党，《TVBS周刊》记者求证民进党部，确实查到一位住北投的陈信宏党员，信息和阿信吻合。五月天和经纪公司从来没正面否认过，只是说，关心的是音乐而不是党员身份。民进党党纲第一条基本主张：
**建 立主权独立自主的台湾共和国**（从1986年成立到现在这条没有改过）。

  

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-ae4bb513c182235a872b060cb3b6027c_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='500'%20height='797'></svg>)

  

③五月天曾经多次参加民进党的党庆晚会，后来因为" **阿
妹效应**"（2000年歌手张惠妹在"总统"就职典礼上唱"国歌"后被取消大陆演唱会），五月天所属唱片公司担心参加民进党党庆活动演出，会让五月天在大陆的演唱会横生枝节变数，于是开始推辞民进党的演出。对五月天无法替民进党党庆晚会演出，民进党中央对外的说法，是五月天无法在928当天排出演出档期。据台媒报道，虽然无法顺利在民进党党庆晚会演出，但五月天还是透过管道向民进党表达，日后还愿在其他民进党活动上表演。

④五月天团员崇拜陈水扁，是 **挺
扁的中坚力量**，给陈水扁站过台。陈水扁也曾出席他们的演唱会，给五月天打气。有知乎网友表示曾经看过一盒早年的五月天台版磁带，纸脊上写着繁体字的"仅以此专辑献给陈水扁总统"。网上还有五月天和陈水扁的亲密合照。

有人洗地说，五月天事先并不知道陈水扁上台后会贪污，巴拉巴拉。我想说，这跟陈水扁贪污有什么关系？陈水扁又没贪污大陆人民的税金，陈水扁的问题是台独好吗？陈水扁又不是上台后才加入民进党和绿营，民进党的台独主张可是写进党纲的，五月天不知道吗？

  

![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/v2-0a1921ad4e55787696b207b2f5821163_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1920'%20height='1080'></svg>)![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-d69328dd8a7ef079157430762656b0be_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='500'%20height='435'></svg>)![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-40d6a63ba790a05e86d507293d16ac8d_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='500'%20height='464'></svg>)![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-26fdb2e546fb71684e7aac55414a7d95_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='500'%20height='339'></svg>)

  

⑤2014年3月19日凌晨，五月天在Facebook贴出歌曲《 **起
来**》的MV，暗示支持反对服贸的民众，引起粉丝疯狂留言，短短10分钟就已累积破千个赞，并有数十个转发。五月天成员玛莎在华山艺文中心开设的咖啡店员工也加入声援行
**反
服贸**的行列，宣布临时店休，告示上写道，"很抱歉，我们不能为了这么点营业额而牺牲了台湾的未来。"并顺势邀请看到告示的民众，一起前往"立法院"参加抗议。

有人说脸书上的图片是五月天的粉丝冒名发的，咖啡店的告示是员工私自贴的，整件事跟玛莎和五月天的其他成员无关，事情是不是真如所说，旁人当然无法求证，然而问题的关键并不在此。

太阳花不仅在大陆是政治不正确，在台湾也属于违法行为。你的粉丝，你的员工，利用你的影响力，去煽动攻占"立法院"，反对两岸服贸， **事 先不知情**就算了，
**事 后也不处理**？明星代言假冒伪劣商品尚且要负连带责任，更何况是具有台独性质的违法活动，你跟我说玛莎和五月天都是无辜的？

至于五月天 **反 核**什么的就不多说了，虽然大陆不具备"用爱发电"的先进技术，但只要你不在大陆反核就好，反正最后缺电的也不是我们。

  

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-217f51281dc62add63d81f1d2dd2a94a_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='600'%20height='412'></svg>)

  

⑥不知道大家还记得周子瑜和戴立忍事件吗？周子瑜发道歉视频，那一句"我是中国人，世界上只有一个中国"说的多么不情不愿。戴立忍发声明自我辩解，绕来绕去，就是不敢说一句"我是中国人"。早些年，在台湾说自己是中国人还是一件很正常的事情，李登辉蔡英文曾经都说过自己是中国人。近些年敢公开宣称自己是中国人那真是需要勇气，台湾的政治环境二十年来严重恶化。远离政治，安心艺术的台湾艺人，我相信大多数人都会表示理解和尊重，不会要求他们站队，表明政治立场。

虽然说每一个人都有参与政治的权利，但权利和义务是一体两面的，既然参与了台独活动，总得 **承
担相应后果**。总不能你去参与台独的时候，说艺人也有表达政治立场的权利，轮到你承担相应后果的时候，却说音乐无关政治。

台独艺人多是在台湾土生土长的娱乐圈人士，他们的行为表现或为岛内的绿军宣传造势；或者间接表明了立场，但多数则掩盖得很好，至少因为他们还不愿意放弃大陆广阔的市场。虽然许多大陆五月天的忠实粉丝仍不相信五月天是台独，并在各大社交圈和网站中努力洗白。然而能证明五月天是台独的新闻层出不穷，粉丝们的洗白也无济于事。

⑦经常有一些五月天的粉丝拿在鸟巢开过演唱会和上过央视来试图洗白五月天不是台独，这种说辞用来骗自己就算了。鸟巢和央视确实都是一些比较重要的场合，安全工作比较严格，需要安检。安检是什么，
**安
检是安全检查，不是政治审查**。鸟巢和央视都是对外开放的公众场合，需要安全检查，不需要政治审查。这是典型的偷换概念。这种说辞只能说明五月天（当时）不是恐怖分子，和五月天台独分子的政治立场毫不相干。

  

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-6d0a2f60fc05c9dcd3fcf1b2e60d001c_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='540'%20height='542'></svg>)

  

[http://m.sohu.com/n/273140946
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//m.sohu.com/n/273140946)  

 ** 演唱会是商业行为**，自负盈亏，你见过做生意去登记还需要调查祖宗八代的吗？又不是敏感或特殊行业。

  

![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-a807bbab766206db3b37c0a20392ab35_hd.png)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1080'%20height='1438'></svg>)

[http://review.jschina.com.cn/redianhuati/201704/t20170426_416422.shtml
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//review.jschina.com.cn/redianhuati/201704/t20170426_416422.shtml)

有粉丝拿来央视节目的截图，说你看五月天说自己来自中国台湾，上面有字幕，我没能找到原始视频出处。但我们都知道央视有一个好习惯，那就是 **会
在字幕中的香港澳门台湾前面冠以中国二字**，不管嘉宾本来说的是台湾，还是中国台湾。至于原因，你懂的。

不知道大家还记不记得去年（2016年）被央视全程打马赛克的香港艺人王喜，还有很久没有消息的毕福剑毕姥爷。

  

![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a2c47c4cc506874673e572b40d05e6d0_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='436'%20height='357'></svg>)

  

央视是党和政府的喉舌，担负政治任务不错。但央视还是电视台，负有娱乐大众的基本功能， **央
视不为任何艺人个人或团队的政治立场背书**。对不起，这口锅央视不背。  

李晶玉也能上央视，但这说明不了她不是台独分子。五月天同样也不能。

  

![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/v2-255ea1dd64255ac641c443230ec91f6a_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='372'%20height='267'></svg>)

  

  

![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-f85b427338d6da269daceabbf3dfcd25_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='640'%20height='1136'></svg>)

⑧有粉丝告诉我五月天在大陆做过慈善，首先对所有参与慈善事业的人表示感激，但是这跟五月天是台独并不冲突。明星也是需要营造个人形象的，这年头明星做慈善不是新闻，从来不做慈善的明星才是新闻。

⑨有歌迷说五月天也说过自己是中国乐队，然而这并不能说明五月天不是台独，只能说明五月天在台独问题上是明知故犯。从李登辉到陈水扁再到蔡英文，哪个没有说过自己是中国人，哪个又不是台独分子？  

  
![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/v2-babade29abe7be12c347cce9a5eb975d_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='554'%20height='317'></svg>)（2000年，时任台湾当局陆委会主委的蔡英文在台湾"立法院"接受"立法委员"质询时，声称自己是中国人）

汪精卫还说自己是"曲线救国"呢？干的却是卖国的勾当。五月天参与台独集会，支持台独政党和政客，阻挠两岸服贸协议，这是中国人该有的行为吗？

## [暴走大事件 片尾曲 抄袭了么？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/39236705/answer/80565811)
\-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------  
以下为2016年5月25日补充答案：  
  
2016版的《暴走大事件主题曲》已经出炉，试听地址可以上我的微博，如下：  
[http://weibo.com/p/10151501_100352525
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//weibo.com/p/10151501_100352525)  
节 目里也已经更新。谢谢所有关注的朋友~~~~  
新版本词曲不变，编曲伴奏全部由我本人创作和演奏~~~不再存在任何疑义。  
旧的版本作为MIXTAPE，无任何商业使用，依然可以在我的微博音乐人里收听。  
\-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------  
  
谢邀，这个应该解释一下。  
  
在说唱圈，通常把伴奏称为BEAT。很多说唱歌手在做MIXTAPE的时候，采样甚至直接使用别人的BEAT，重新更换歌词作为自己的作品，是说唱圈常有的事，也是全世界说唱文化的一部分。但是MIXTAPE和原创是不一样的，通常不能用于商业，只用于地下传播或网络传播。  
  
可以参考百度百科MIXTAPE：  
[mixtape_百度百科
__](https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//baike.baidu.com/link%3Furl
%3DIT5Dx-LoWKSVP-DhgEmGABExElA9-JxCjDutgBVGPyD1PP-
2A20UFi7ybsbft_3S9Nl_KXiyoYn-27QeFfqdSa)  
"
若不用于商业盈利，Mixtape可以免费使用任何歌曲的伴奏加以混音、衔接，唱入自己的歌词将原歌曲再版，它的重点在于其歌词内容和思想，这种随意又自由的方式是说唱歌手"练嘴"与宣传的最佳途径"  
  
比如早期EMINEM的很多歌，用的也都是Dre的Beat，后来很多说唱歌手包括国内的一些说唱RAPPER也大量使用Em的Beat。比如小驴TOMMY著名的《十元人民币》，最初版就用的EMINEM的伴奏，不过他在专辑版本里重新制作了BEAT，没有继续使用EM的原版伴奏。东北说唱歌手葡桃的《留学垃圾》就用的热狗的原版伴奏。另外国内还有首很著名的说唱  
歌曲《大学自习室》，作者叫郝雨，那首歌的伴奏也是直接用的cmcb乐队的《第一次亲密接触之板砖脸》。  
  
百度的rap吧，有个置顶帖对此的态度是：用别人的Beat不是一件丢脸的事，但用自己的Beat绝对是一件很光荣的事。  
  
这首歌当时接到任务，时间紧，我来不及做BEAT，就找到了这首歌，将它的伴奏作为素材，重新做了剪辑，作为《暴走大事件》的BEAT重新写了歌曲和旋律。从说唱圈的角度来说，是可以接受的，当时也是把暴走大事件作为网络节目，并没想太多，我也只是想做一首MIXTAPE里收录的作品。不过现在暴走大事件已经渐渐不再只是网络节目，我也希望在今年能够重新花时间制作一版新的原创BEAT，录一个正式版的《暴走大事件主题曲》。  
  
总结，目前大家听到的暴走大事件主题曲，作词作曲是我，编曲是freestyle。  
不过这个BEAT的使用，确实也没和原作者报备，这个错在我。所以虽然不属抄袭，但也得算不合法借用BEAT。  
  
我当时为暴走创作这首歌，并未收取任何费用，纯粹以兴趣帮忙，所以也没考虑太多。既然有朋友提到这个，考虑到暴走大事件现在的收视率，也确实应该重新编一个原创的BEAT重录这首歌了，我会努力滴~~~~


## [《中国好声音第四季》的张姝说自己3岁就喜欢看书，这是一种怎样的体验？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/33780038/answer/66606559)
大半夜上知乎搜了一下自己的名字，看到了这个问题。好多人在微博上问我也懒得回答。今天就解读一下这件事。  
我从小属于那种精力旺盛型的小孩，对世界一直保持一种带有敬畏的好奇心，观察蚂蚁什么的也不会拿放大镜烧焦的那种。我是老来子，父母年纪很大观念很旧都有很好的读书习惯，而且我所有的表哥表姐都比我大很多岁，从小第一个高端![](https://pic4.zhimg.com/50/532bc07e135cc79b27738801ad039703_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='3264'%20height='2448'></svg>)的人生体验就是没人愿意陪我玩导致的寂寞。一直以来家里都有很多书，一开始是一岁的时候妈妈给读书听，但是我妈有个不良嗜好就是超级爱打麻将。所以那个三百六十五天每天的小故事只读了几天她就给我丢一边了，加之没有玩伴陪玩，电视不让我看没人给我买玩具，出门玩又不让因为太小，所有的娱乐世界就是读书，于是我学会了查字典。先从童话入手，后来翻着家里的连环画看。结果连环画不全你懂的，三国水浒西游和东周列国志的情节完全接不上，刚刚还在晋文公，就给我直接跳到了楚怀王。对于好奇心过旺从小强迫症的我来说是种残酷的打击。在我死皮赖脸连哭带作之后我妈一发善心给我买了一套吉林文史出版社的古典文学集。当时第一本读的的确是西游记，然后我就掉进去出不来了。三国、水浒、东周列国志、三侠五义、红楼梦（这些书在后来的岁月里也在反复读，少说读了五六遍，多说就不提了）……比较坑爹的是后来读三言二拍的时候是非删节版。那个醒世恒言里的乔太守乱点鸳鸯谱，金海陵纵欲身亡对我的性教育启蒙有了毁灭性的打击。不过从苏小妹三难新郎里我开始迷恋古诗词。于是反过来把红楼梦里的诗词反反复复的读，开始没完没了的背诗。古代的诗词歌赋有一种奇妙的韵律感，和音乐是不谋而合的。我的学霸爹（他是学霸我真不是）看我悟性不错，于是搞来了四书五经。小学五年级之前的生活基本上就是不停的背，没别的原因就是喜欢。后来开始从钢铁是怎样炼成的开始读老外名著……市面上的人民文学出版社出的那一套书基本没有没看过的，这一点可以向我当年的所有语文老师求证他们对我真是又爱又恨上课跟老师较真顶嘴不是一次两次了。因为爹妈年纪大，所以红色文学如暴风骤雨、太阳照在桑干河上、山乡巨变、冯德英的三《花》、林海雪原、红岩、大刀记诸如此类的那时候让我翻烂了，毛泽东诗词拿来狂背，陈毅的诗词就喜欢梅岭三章。所以早些年活得是根正苗红差点发展成中二青年。直到后来读了家里那套老掉牙的鲁迅全集，我开始一个作家一个作家的读……余华、金庸、贾平凹、莫言、村上春树……还会把诺贝尔文学奖的获奖者的书、茅盾文学奖获奖书籍一本一本拿来看。现代诗歌也看了一部分，希梅内斯浪漫的我起了一身鸡皮疙瘩，推理小说我是新本格狂热粉，宋词我喜欢晏几道，元曲就爱那段窦娥冤，奇词怪句我喜欢赏花归去马如飞，道光茶壶也不错，我时常会被侠之大者感化的情操翻涌，也会被小情小爱折磨的彻夜难眠，甚至痴迷地图册和辞海，因为这世界里所有的未知我都想了解。大学时期学了法学因为超级爱看书，但是因为一直要在音乐和专业上摇摆加上我超级讨厌教科书所以考研各种不顺利，乐队和驻唱占用了我大块的时间但是读书却没停过。读书从来不是为了黄金屋、颜如玉、千钟粟，开始只是一点小小的好奇心、占据童年的寂寞和一屋子的爹妈读过的书，到后来演变成了将会陪伴我一生的的习惯。现在因为经常飞来飞去赶通告我买了个kindle，参加比赛阶段读完了马伯庸和冯唐……很多人去质疑我三岁读书的真实性，第一我想说没有的人觉得你是在炫耀而拥有的人会觉得你是在陈述，第二如果你想让未来的小孩多读书最好的办法就是培养出来他的强迫症然后把他丢到一本读了一半的书旁边再丢一本字典给他。试问世界上哪个牛掰的作家不是从小读书读书破万卷我这才哪到哪，世人接受不了的不是有人可以如此爱书，只是接受不了我一个玩音乐的如此爱书而已。没什么不可能的，世界很大，出去看看吧。  
还有啊，跑来说看懂看不懂的，我觉得一定不是读书人，什么叫看懂，读到几分算是看懂，标准是如何界定的？我自己看我自己的，你管我懂不懂。还真是智者见智，仁者见仁，那啥只能看到那啥。还是那句话，没什么不可能的，世界很大，出去看看吧。  
![](https://pic2.zhimg.com/50/b620c6804bb1418e1164df1d032ac6dd_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='964'%20height='1286'></svg>)  
性别不明的贴张图自己辨别吧，算不上颜值担当，抱歉给哈林组拖后腿了。![](https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/ce459aea9beda0843019f211b8d269b0_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='480'%20height='640'></svg>)  
![](https://pic3.zhimg.com/50/3fa2fa66245a4873fcfc4db7f852a37e_hd.jpg)![](data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20width='1280'%20height='1280'></svg>)  
我恨十六比九。


## [民谣歌手是如何创作的？](https://www.zhihu.com/question/27405321/answer/36507710)
早上10点起床。  
在厕所蹲坑的时候，脑子里忽然响起一段调调，嘴里哼出来。  
然后反复哼上几遍，怕擦完屁股就忘了。  
副歌哼差不多了，用吉他试几个高难度和弦组合：C，Am。 F，G，尼玛听起来真和谐，我简直是天才。  
然后出去喝一碗胡辣汤，吃5块钱的煎包。  
回来刷刷微博，抠抠脚，打打游戏，一下子就到了傍晚。  
接着手机响了，音乐圈儿的朋友叫去喝酒。  
到了酒吧老板说，怎么又迟到了，鼓手来了好久了。  
然后拿着一瓶酒上台，开场唱一首无节操的搞笑歌曲。第一句刚唱完，突然停下，不好意思，忘记调弦了。  
几首唱过，嗓子口干舌燥。走到吧台休息一下，想起早上写了一半的歌，老板，给我纸笔。然后绞尽脑汁，先写几个押韵的词作为每句的结尾，"故乡""远方""姑娘""忧伤"，然后绞尽脑汁，再从大脑歌词库中找词把他们串在一起。  
然后重新上台：各位，今天是个平凡的日子，但是你们能来到这里，就是不平凡的，因为我刚刚写了一首歌，从来没有演出过，现在我就把它献给各位，献给所有在旅途中漂泊的人们，献给所有在风中飘荡的答案。希望你们能够喜欢。  
鼓手，给我一个4/4拍。  
 _沉 默的云彩下是我沉默的故乡  
那里是否还有我深爱的姑娘  
那年我一言不发地走向远方  
留下她独自倾诉着忧伤  
#%*（**（）*（*￥￥%￥#  
34…￥%*（&（）（）%…234%  
%23&…！！#…&*&234…  
…45&*…878、&456…&*…456*（总共重复3遍，最后一遍开始扯着嗓子并且扫弦）_  
谢谢。  
观众：唔----，牛屄----，好听----、  
心中顿时满足了。高兴，喝得上吐下泻。被人抬回家。  
第二天早上11点，醒来以后，蹲在马桶上。  
诶，昨晚那首歌怎么唱的来着？
